You can play it alone against one to three computer opponents or with a group of friends or family.  \r\n\r\nIn Ludo Supremo you must move all of your pieces from your yard into your home area. The first player to do so wins. To enter a piece into play from its yard to its starting square, a player must roll a 6. If a player has no pieces in play they get 3 tries to get a 6. Once a player has one or more pieces in play, he selects a piece and moves it forward along the track the number of squares indicated by the die roll.
